<p style="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in">Item
8.01 Other Events</p>

<p style="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 9.35pt">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">On May 5, 2023, Comcast Corporation (&#8220;Comcast&#8221;)
announced the pricing terms of its previously announced cash tender offers (together with the Floating Rate Offer (as defined below),
the &#8220;Comcast Offers&#8221;) to purchase any and all of its outstanding 3.700% Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;3.700% Notes&#8221;) and
any and all of its outstanding 3.375% Notes due 2025 (the &#8220;3.375% Notes&#8221;), and Sky Limited, a subsidiary of Comcast (&#8220;Sky&#8221;
and, together with Comcast, the &#8220;Issuers&#8221;), announced the pricing terms of its previously announced cash tender offer (the
&#8220;Sky Offer&#8221; and, together with the Comcast Offers, the &#8220;Offers&#8221;) to purchase any and all of its outstanding 3.750%
Senior Unsecured Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;3.750% Notes&#8221; and, together with the 3.375% Notes and the 3.700% Notes, the &#8220;Fixed
Rate Notes&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Comcast previously announced the consideration
for its outstanding Floating Rate Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;Floating Rate Notes&#8221; and, together with the Fixed Rate Notes, the &#8220;Notes&#8221;)
validly tendered and accepted for purchase pursuant to Comcast&#8217;s cash tender offer (the &#8220;Floating Rate Offer&#8221;) to purchase
any and all of its outstanding Floating Rate Notes.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The Offers were announced on May 1, 2023,
and were made pursuant to the Offer to Purchase and the related Notice of Guaranteed Delivery, each dated May 1, 2023 (the &#8220;Tender
Offer Documents&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">On May 8, 2023, the Issuers announced the
results of the Offers.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Copies of Comcast&#8217;s press releases relating
to the pricing and results of the Offers are attached as Exhibits 99.1 and 99.2 hereto and are incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">This Current Report on Form 8-K is
neither an offer to sell nor a solicitation of offers to buy any securities. The Offers were made only pursuant to the Tender Offer
Documents. The Offers were not made to holders of securities in any jurisdiction in which the making or acceptance thereof would not
be in compliance with the securities, blue sky or other laws of such jurisdiction.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

9.01 Exhibits</p>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Comcast Corporation
and Sky Limited Announce Pricing Terms of Offers to Purchase Certain of their Outstanding Senior Debt Securities</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">May 5, 2023 12:00 PM Eastern Daylight
Time</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">PHILADELPHIA--(BUSINESS WIRE)--Comcast
Corporation (&ldquo;<B>Comcast</B>&rdquo;) today announced the pricing terms of its previously announced cash tender offers to purchase
any and all of its outstanding 3.700% Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;<B>3.700% Notes</B>&rdquo;) and any and all of its outstanding 3.375%
Notes due 2025 (the &ldquo;<B>3.375% Notes</B>&rdquo;) and Sky Limited, a subsidiary of Comcast (&ldquo;<B>Sky</B>&rdquo; and, together
with Comcast, the &ldquo;<B>Issuers</B>&rdquo;) today announced the pricing terms of its previously announced cash tender offer to purchase
any and all of its outstanding 3.750% Senior Unsecured Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;<B>3.750% Notes</B>&rdquo; and, together with the 3.375%
Notes and the 3.700% Notes, the &ldquo;<B>Fixed Rate Notes</B>&rdquo;).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">As previously announced, Comcast is
also offering $1,006 per $1,000 principal amount of its outstanding Floating Rate Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;<B>Floating Rate Notes</B>&rdquo;
and, together with the Fixed Rate Notes, the &ldquo;<B>Notes</B>&rdquo;) validly tendered and accepted for purchase pursuant to Comcast&rsquo;s
cash tender offer to purchase any and all of its outstanding Floating Rate Notes.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The consideration offered per $1,000
principal amount of Notes validly tendered and accepted for purchase pursuant to the applicable offers is set forth in the table below:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(1)</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Per $1,000 principal amount of Notes validly
                                            tendered before the Expiration Time (as defined below), not validly withdrawn and accepted
                                            for purchase. In addition to the applicable consideration, all holders whose Notes are accepted
                                            for purchase will also receive accrued and unpaid interest on such Notes from, and including,
                                            the last interest payment date up to, but excluding, the Settlement Date (as defined below).</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The consideration offered per $1,000
principal amount of Fixed Rate Notes validly tendered and accepted for purchase pursuant to the applicable offers was determined by the
Joint Dealer Managers referred to below in the manner described in the Offer to Purchase (as defined below) by reference to the applicable
fixed spread specified above for such series of Fixed Rate Notes</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">plus the yield based on the applicable
bid-side price of the Treasury Reference Security specified above for such series of Fixed Rate Notes as quoted on the Bloomberg Reference
Page specified above for such series of Fixed Rate Notes as of 11:00 a.m., New York City time today.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The tender offers will expire at 5:00
p.m., New York City time, on May 5, 2023, unless extended or earlier terminated (the &ldquo;<B>Expiration Time</B>&rdquo;). Holders who
have validly tendered their Notes may withdraw such Notes at any time at or prior to the Expiration Time. The Guaranteed Delivery Date
is May 9, 2023. The Issuers expect to pay the applicable consideration for Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior
to the Expiration Time on May 10, 2023, the third business day following the Expiration Time (the &ldquo;<B>Settlement Date</B>&rdquo;).
The tender offers are conditioned upon satisfaction of certain conditions, but are not conditioned upon any minimum amount of Notes being
tendered.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

the tender offers are set forth in the Offer to Purchase, dated May 1, 2023 (the &ldquo;<B>Offer to Purchase</B>&rdquo;) and in the related
Notice of Guaranteed Delivery, along with any amendments and supplements thereto, which holders are urged to read carefully before making
any decision with respect to the tender offers. The Issuers have retained Deutsche Bank Securities Inc. and TD Securities (USA) LLC to
act as Joint Dealer Managers in connection with the tender offers. Copies of the Offer to Purchase and the related Notice of Guaranteed
Delivery may be obtained from D.F. King &amp; Co., Inc., the Tender and Information Agent for the tender offers, by phone at +1 (212)
269-5550 (banks and brokers) or +1 (877) 487-5045 (all others), by email at cmcsa@dfking.com or online at https://www.dfking.com/cmcsa.
Questions regarding the tender offers may also be directed to the Joint Dealer Managers as set forth below:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">About Comcast Corporation</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">Comcast Corporation
(Nasdaq: CMCSA) is a global media and technology company. From the connectivity and platforms we provide, to the content and experiences
we create, our businesses </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Comcast Corporation
and Sky Limited Announce Results of Tender Offers for Certain of their Outstanding Senior Debt Securities</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">May 8, 2023</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">PHILADELPHIA--(BUSINESS
WIRE)--Comcast Corporation (&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Comcast<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;) announced the
results, as of 5:00 p.m., New York City time, on May 5, 2023 (the &ldquo;</FONT>Expiration Time<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;),
of its previously announced cash tender offers for its outstanding 3.700% Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;</FONT>3.700% Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;),
its outstanding Floating Rate Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;</FONT>Floating Rate Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;) and its
outstanding 3.375% Notes due 2025 (the &ldquo;</FONT>3.375% Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo; and, together with the 3.700%
Notes and the Floating Rate Notes, the &ldquo;</FONT>Comcast Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;) and Sky Limited, a subsidiary
of Comcast (&ldquo;</FONT>Sky<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo; and, together with Comcast, the &ldquo;</FONT>Issuers<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;),
announced the results, as of the Expiration Time, of its previously announced cash tender offer for its outstanding 3.750% Senior Unsecured
Notes due 2024 (the &ldquo;</FONT>3.750% Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo; and, together with the Comcast Notes, the &ldquo;</FONT>Notes<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;).
The cash tender offers were announced on May 1, 2023 and were made pursuant to the Offer to Purchase and the related Notice of Guaranteed
Delivery, each dated May 1, 2023 (the &ldquo;</FONT>Tender Offer Documents<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;). The following table
presents the aggregate principal amount of the Notes tendered and not validly withdrawn as of the Expiration Time and the aggregate principal
amount of the Notes tendered pursuant to the guaranteed delivery procedures described in the Tender Offer Documents. </FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">Comcast has accepted
for purchase all Comcast Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior to the Expiration Time and Sky has accepted for
purchase all 3.750% Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior to the Expiration Time. Holders whose Notes have been
accepted for purchase will also receive accrued and unpaid interest on the purchased Notes from, and including, the last interest payment
date for such Notes up to, but excluding, the Settlement Date (as defined below). The Issuers also expect to accept Notes validly tendered
and delivered pursuant to the guaranteed delivery procedures described in the Tender Offer Documents. The Issuers will not accept any
further tenders.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">The settlement
date for Notes validly tendered and not validly withdrawn at or prior to the Expiration Time is expected to be May 10, 2023 (the &ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Settlement
Date<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;). On May 1, 2023, Comcast priced an offering of $5.0 billion aggregate principal amount
of new notes (the &ldquo;</FONT>New Notes Offering<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&rdquo;). The New Notes Offering is expected to close
on May 9, 2023, subject to customary closing conditions. Comcast intends to use all or a portion of the net proceeds from the New Notes
Offering to fund the purchase of the Comcast Notes. Sky intends to fund the purchase of the 3.750% Notes with cash on hand. </FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">Deutsche Bank Securities
Inc. and TD Securities (USA) LLC served as Joint Dealer Managers for the tender offer.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">This news release
is neither an offer to purchase nor a solicitation of an offer to sell any securities. The tender offers were made only by, and pursuant
to the terms of, the Tender Offer Documents. The tender offers were not made in any jurisdiction in which the making or acceptance thereof
would not be in compliance with the securities, blue sky or other laws of such jurisdiction. In any jurisdiction where the laws require
the tender offers to be made by a licensed broker or dealer, the tender offers were made by the Joint Dealer Managers on behalf of the
Issuers. None of the Issuers, the Tender and Information Agent or the Joint Dealer Managers, nor any of their affiliates, has made any
recommendation as to whether holders should tender or refrain from tendering all or any portion of their Notes in response to the tender
offers.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">About Comcast Corporation</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">Comcast Corporation
(Nasdaq: CMCSA) is a global media and technology company. From the connectivity and platforms we provide, to the content and experiences
we create, our businesses reach hundreds of millions of customers, viewers, and guests worldwide. We deliver world-class broadband, wireless,
and video through Xfinity, Comcast Business, and Sky; produce, distribute, and stream leading entertainment, sports, and news through
brands including NBC, Telemundo, Universal, Peacock, and Sky; and bring incredible theme parks and attractions to life through Universal
Destinations &amp; Experiences. Visit www.comcastcorporation.com for more information.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">Caution Concerning Forward-Looking
Statements</FONT></P>

including the risks and uncertainties we describe in the &ldquo;Risk Factors&rdquo; sections of our most recent Annual Report on Form
10-K, our most recent Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q and other reports filed with the </FONT></P>
